        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer263365054" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7452675324383083552">Another fabulous installment in the Rock Chick series, and I do believe that Jules is a close runner up to Jet in my favorite Rock Chick spot. She's a social worker with an attitude. After losing her entire family as a child, she's now unwittingly made her own. Between her boys on the street that she protects nightly, her new found Rock Chick friends, and of course, the hot pack, you would think that she would be well insulated from the drug lords of Denver. But Jules is the toughest Rock Chick </span>
  <span id="freeText7452675324383083552" style="display:none">Another fabulous installment in the Rock Chick series, and I do believe that Jules is a close runner up to Jet in my favorite Rock Chick spot. She's a social worker with an attitude. After losing her entire family as a child, she's now unwittingly made her own. Between her boys on the street that she protects nightly, her new found Rock Chick friends, and of course, the hot pack, you would think that she would be well insulated from the drug lords of Denver. But Jules is the toughest Rock Chick there is. I usually go for the helpless females, hence my love of the dominating males. But Jules had an innate vulnerability that she covered up with attitude. <br /><br />I love Jules' internal dialogue. Her nickname for her inner ass kicker is 'head bashing mamma jamma.' I laughed every single time. She also talks to her cat. He answers in meows, but she knows what he's saying. And being an animal lover myself, I know how it is when you know your pet to that extreme. Could be a little scary for people who don't know you. But Vance takes it in stride and in fact, this is one of Jules endearing qualities. What a guy!<br /><br />Vance at first just tries to make her see reason, and when Jules teenage boys from the foster home are threatened, he finally steps up and helps out. Only he falls just about as fast as the rest of the hot pack and their women. So he changes tactics, and sets about wooing Jules "Kristen Ashley" style. You know, the style that would make me kick his a** to the curb in real life, but makes me swoon to read about.<br /><br />This is the first KA book that has made me cry. Maybe because, while the other men and women are fabulous together and one hundred percent dedicated to each other, Jules and Vance are the first couple that truly <i>needs</i> each other. Their story is, as always hilarious but also heartfelt and suspenseful. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7452675324383083552" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_280350694" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/280350694" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/280350694?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=private-investigator-hero">private-investigator-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=native-american-hero">native-american-hero</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280350694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2647367100347975204">We pick up the action in this one minutes after <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9799572.Rock_Chick_Redemption__Rock_Chick___3_' title='Rock Chick Redemption (Rock Chick, #3) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rock Chick Redemption</a> left off with Vance in hot pursuit of Jules on his Harley after watching her shoot out a drug dealer’s tyres right in front of Fortnums. Jules is a social worker by day and avenging angel vigilante by night. She works at a shelter for homeless kids and is hellbent on revenge after finding one of her boys dead of an OD with a syringe lying by his body.<br/><br/>She’s a girl who has loved and lost nearly her entire family. Her parents and</span>
  <span id="freeText2647367100347975204" style="display:none">We pick up the action in this one minutes after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9799572.Rock_Chick_Redemption__Rock_Chick___3_" title="Rock Chick Redemption (Rock Chick, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick Redemption</a> left off with Vance in hot pursuit of Jules on his Harley after watching her shoot out a drug dealer’s tyres right in front of Fortnums. Jules is a social worker by day and avenging angel vigilante by night. She works at a shelter for homeless kids and is hellbent on revenge after finding one of her boys dead of an OD with a syringe lying by his body.<br /><br />She’s a girl who has loved and lost nearly her entire family. Her parents and brother were killed in a car crash when she was small and she now shares a duplex with Nick, the widower of her aunt, her last surviving relative, who died when she was 15. She’s scared to let herself care for anyone because she’s known the acute pain of loss and doesn’t want to experience it again. She now lives with and talks daily to her kittycat Boo, not to be confused with the Boo that prowls the corridors of the Brotherhood Mansion.<br /><br />Vance is one of Lee’s boys, of Native American descent. He’s drop dead gorgeous with a fall of glossy black hair and Jules is deeply attracted to him right from the get go. Lee and his crew have all heard of her antics and, whilst disapproving of her lone ranger act, do approve of her campaign and decide to let it be known that she has their protection.<br /><br />The love story really takes centre stage in this one with everyone warning Jules that Vance is a P-L-A-Y-E-R and with her reluctance to give into her feelings. Vance makes a romantic gesture on her birthday and she completely freaks and pushes him away. She was beginning to annoy me by then and I felt sorry for Vance. Enter Luke – she has a little dalliance with him (who wouldn’t??) and Vance really doesn’t like it and their relationship starts to come together.<br /><br />They’re very sweet together and I loved their romance. The suspense plot simmers gently in the background in this one with the burgeoning relationship between Jules and Vance coming to the fore and it is beautiful the way she lets down her inner defences and slowly lets him in. Eventually, the suspense plot bursts into life in a more dramatic and explosive way than any other Rock Chick novel with the most intense ending with every Rock Chick getting a moment to reflect on what is happening.<br /><br />All the usual crew are here and it’s another rich walk through the lush countryside which is Rock Chick World. We end with a little hint of the next novel which will undoubtedly involve Luke, who I confess to having a bit of a crush on!!<br /><br />5 stars – romantic suspense.<br /><br />I wanted to add this as a quote but decided it was too spoilerific so....<br /><br />Beware............here be spoilers<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ As Jules is recovering from being shot in the chest and the abdomen, she's wary of getting naked with Vance again and resuming their sex life because of her scars. I loved this scene between the pair of them.<br /><br /><i>“I… you… well…” I stopped then started again, “it’s pretty clear you’re the kind of guy who has to have sex, um… a lot of it and, um… we can’t have sex anymore.”<br /><br />“Why can’t we have sex anymore?”<br /><br />“Well,” I started and halted. Did I really have to explain it?<br />I looked at him. He was glaring at me.<br />I guessed I did.<br /><br />“I’m kind of gross,” I finished.<br /><br />“Gross?”<br /><br />“Yes, gross.”<br /><br />“How are you gross?”<br /><br />Now I was getting pissed. “I can’t believe you’re gonna make me spell it out for you,” I snapped.<br /><br />His hand moved, it went down over my hip then up under my shirt then both his arms wrapped around me. “He could have blown off half your face, you survived, you’d still be lyin’ beside me.”<br />I blinked.<br /><br />He didn’t pause for me to wrap my head around that mind-blowing statement, he went on. “One of those bullets could have torn through your spinal cord, you’d be lyin’ beside me.”<br /><br />Oh my God.<br /><br />His arms got tighter, pressing my body against his and his face came super-close. “This is it. You and me. No matter what,” he said.<br />“Crowe –” I whispered, so stunned, so moved, I thought my heart had to have stopped beating.<br /><br />“No matter what,” he said, his voice fierce and strong and rumbling through me. “You told me I was home to you and I get it. You’re home to me. I’ve never had a home. I like the one I found and I’m not losin’ it. No matter what.”</i>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Le sigh!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2647367100347975204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_977321798" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/977321798" />
    <a title="Pam Nelson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15402332-pam-nelson"><img alt="Pam Nelson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544491116p2/15402332.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/977321798?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam Nelson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam Nelson" href="/user/show/15402332-pam-nelson">Pam Nelson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22518371-rock-chick-renegade">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=_finished-2017">_finished-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=_finished-2014">_finished-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer977321798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11312726565329396412">Just as witty and funny as the last 3 books love this series! Can't wait to keep reading. I do wish one of the crew would get with Jane the quiet book chick... just wishful thinking :) - 5th time <br/><br/>5 Renegade Stars <br/><br/>This is a great addition to this series to be for sure. Who isn’t entranced by Vance? He hasn’t had an easy life but things got a lot better when he started working for Lee.<br/><br/>Jules is her own brand of crazy, but you gotta love the girl. She sure brings out some spice; nothing is boring wi</span>
  <span id="freeText11312726565329396412" style="display:none">Just as witty and funny as the last 3 books love this series! Can't wait to keep reading. I do wish one of the crew would get with Jane the quiet book chick... just wishful thinking :) - 5th time <br /><br />5 Renegade Stars <br /><br />This is a great addition to this series to be for sure. Who isn’t entranced by Vance? He hasn’t had an easy life but things got a lot better when he started working for Lee.<br /><br />Jules is her own brand of crazy, but you gotta love the girl. She sure brings out some spice; nothing is boring with this girl. <br /><br />Jules has had a hard life, losing her family. After a prolonged hospital stays herself, then she goes to live with her Aunt Reba and Nick. But then Reba passes suddenly. It messed with her. She protects herself by building a wall. And has an emotional Rottweiler so no one can hurt her again.<br /><br /><i>‘I was kind of flipping out. This was normal stuff that normal girls do. I’d never been normal. I’d always been kind of a freak.’</i> – Jules <br /><br />So now that she works with runaways and kids on the streets, and when she loses one of her kids to drugs. She kind of went vigilant. She has been messing with the drug dealers and kind of got herself on Sal big drug guys radar. <br /><br />Enter Vance, who also got an eye for Jules. Or The Law as her kids call her. He is not going to back down, oh now he doesn’t; he sees what he wants like all the boys do. He gets under her defenses. Vance’s breaks down the wall and turns her emotional Rottweiler into a cuddle squirmy pug puppy. Also I love that he calls her Princess. Swooon!!<br /><br /><i>‘Nick used to look at Auntie Reba that way. <br />Like she was breath. <br />Like she was necessity. <br />Like she was life. <br />That was the way Vance was looking at me.’</i> - Jules<br /><br />Funny how she has a dog as an emotional barrio but she has the coolest cat Boo, who I just love. I guess because I am a cat person and have 4 of the fur babies I get the cat talking and talking back to them. Cause I sooo do that… Haha. <br /><br />Also got to love the girl posse!! We get all the girls again in this book I think that’s one of the things I like about a Kristen Ashley book, you never feel like you’re missing older characters because they play a role in all the books. <br /><br />I know that I say this with every book, but Susannah Jones kills it with these book, her voices are awesome. I can tell who’s talking just by her voice how cool is that! She really gave each character their own voice. She is one of my most favorite narrators for sure. <br /><br />*All my Reviews are 100% honest and my own.*</span>
  <a data-text-id="11312726565329396412" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1910285695?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1910285695" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer614042520176374880"><b>You know me</b>, then you know I always have a problem with <i>insta-love</i>. If you know me, you also know I (for the most time) a problem with KA's female characters. <b>Juliet 'Jules' "Law" Lawler</b> (26/27) was a alright woman, though a but too naive and stupid that made me eye-rolling my eyes a couple of times. But I liked that she could actually kickass and I liked that she would do anything for her <i>kids</i>. <b>Vance Crowe</b> (30?) was a good, sexy man who saw someone he wanted and he made her his. I do love that </span>
  <span id="freeText614042520176374880" style="display:none"><b>You know me</b>, then you know I always have a problem with <i>insta-love</i>. If you know me, you also know I (for the most time) a problem with KA's female characters. <b>Juliet 'Jules' "Law" Lawler</b> (26/27) was a alright woman, though a but too naive and stupid that made me eye-rolling my eyes a couple of times. But I liked that she could actually kickass and I liked that she would do anything for her <i>kids</i>. <b>Vance Crowe</b> (30?) was a good, sexy man who saw someone he wanted and he made her his. I do love that kind of males. Though Vance wasn't my favorite KA alpha male, he was still awesome. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Home isn’t a place. Home is anywhere, just as long as the people you love are there.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I have to mention that I <i>L O V E</i> <b>Lee Nightingale</b>. And you can help but to adore <b>Lucas Stark</b>. I do really want Lee and his men to protect me. To be around me. I would be in heaven. As far as the story goes, there was a bit more action in this one that the other KA books I've read lately, which is good. I had kinda given up on <b>Rock Chick</b> series after realizing that the Rock Chicks annoyed the living hell out of me, but those damn males keep making me come back for me. I'm even considering re-read Lee's book again...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Wherever it takes me, good to know in the end, it’ll lead back to you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1486921281i/21961373.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series (Standalone), Book Four<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No and yes, as there was a misunderstanding. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Can I say Lee Nightingale?<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes and no. I don't know.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br><b>Rating</b> - 3 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3733940-gretchen-about-that-story?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3733940-gretchen-about-that-story?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100046628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16595005821736105118"><b>Great story! It had everything I've come to love from Kristen Ashley.</b><br/><br/>Jules is fantastic! I mean, seriously, stand up for yourself, take on the world, kick ass and I loved that about her. Her and Vance together were great, he had that awesome alpha male thing going on but gave her a bit more room to be herself it seemed, I liked it a lot. I liked how they met, the growth of their relationship was good even though it was pretty instant. I loved the bickering and sexy times (HOT!). I enjoyed gettin</span>
  <span id="freeText16595005821736105118" style="display:none"><b>Great story! It had everything I've come to love from Kristen Ashley.</b><br /><br />Jules is fantastic! I mean, seriously, stand up for yourself, take on the world, kick ass and I loved that about her. Her and Vance together were great, he had that awesome alpha male thing going on but gave her a bit more room to be herself it seemed, I liked it a lot. I liked how they met, the growth of their relationship was good even though it was pretty instant. I loved the bickering and sexy times (HOT!). I enjoyed getting to know Vance a but I wish there would have been more details about him. <br /><br />Besides the main characters evolving relationship, I also liked the story of Jules and how she was fighting in her vigilante justice type ways. Some parts of the story were pretty funny but it could also be serious and intense, there was a nice balance. Jules at the shelter with the kids was wonderful and heart warming.<br /><br />All the key players from previous stories were in this and I totally enjoyed it. Everything intertwined nicely but this book had a different feel to it for me. It was more about Jules and Vance’s relationship than Rock Chick antics. I was kind of missing some of the fun and laughter, it was there, just not as much. I like that Duke had more of a voice in this and new characters were introduced. Every one of them is so well thought out and detailed. Luke was so sweet in this (he always is!) and I love how protective all the guys get about the women.<br /><br />Excellent drama at the end. Loved how it all wrapped up and I'm super excited for Luke's story next, which was introduced right at the end. He needs a good woman!<br /><br /><b>Great story. Twists and turns with lots of butt-kicking mixed in between the romance. Heartfelt and wonderful!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16595005821736105118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer307656145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9978235182126318855">Vance has seen it all in his life, but he can honestly say he has never seen a vigilante women yielding a gun chasing, a notorious player and thug and looking down right sexy at the same time. As he watches Jules "Law" spring into action he knows two things: 1. She can't go around shooting a gun in public or her work will be for naught. 2. She is his, he plans to claim her in everyway possible, she just doesn't know it yet.<br/><br/>Jules can't help the fluttering feeling she has when around Vance, but sh</span>
  <span id="freeText9978235182126318855" style="display:none">Vance has seen it all in his life, but he can honestly say he has never seen a vigilante women yielding a gun chasing, a notorious player and thug and looking down right sexy at the same time. As he watches Jules "Law" spring into action he knows two things: 1. She can't go around shooting a gun in public or her work will be for naught. 2. She is his, he plans to claim her in everyway possible, she just doesn't know it yet.<br /><br />Jules can't help the fluttering feeling she has when around Vance, but she plans to ignore it, at least after he kisses her. Not one to take orders from anyone, Jules plans to continue her quest for ridding the streets of filth, but when a target is put on her back, Vance steps in. As if it is confusing enough to find she has deep feelings for the man everyone says is a player, the Rock Chicks have claimed her as family and she doesn't know what to do about that either. Well at least with Vance she can think of several things to do and decides maybe she will just go with the flow, even if there is a few hiccups along the way.<br /><br />This is my second favorite in the series so far. Vance is like a smore, ooey and gooey and makes your insides melt. I loved this story, it was a total blast, I could never have imagined a use for saran wrap the way it is used in this book and it is hilarious. Rock on Rock Chicks!</span>

      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/SEzFrDvVsWK47bFv0avgIDmZrtfKF06kWrZgE/Wz0yAEsg3QjLbxtrv6zbBXb069YCq6q7I7O0RPWnsglLyNw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jRV9w1sOnD26fQlYueyjIFyDrc6L6yrFT1lpEJOGkwXwJobiqdMRPupxVKvH97GaKeVhn3oLmxLPDtl8XgKufg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

The last thing she will ever do is ask for someone else’s help. But when that choice is out of her control, forcing her to rely on others to save her and her family, and pick up the pieces that are left, will she be able to let someone else be her strength?\n\nThe second Greg locks eyes with Meli, he knows that she is someone he needs. Someone he craves. Meli knew the second she met Greg that he would be nothing but trouble and heartache. Her life takes an unexpected turn, and that bitch Fate is back to wreak more havoc on another member of the Corps family.\n\nAll hell breaks loose, leaving Greg no choice but to call in a favor. He hooks back up with his old friend Braxxon Breaker from the Breakneck MC. <span id="freeTextContainer12425961834064611783">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText12425961834064611783" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
